	<script type="text/javascript">
		var LangDialogDiv, LangDialog, LangSelectForm, LangInfoDiv;
		$(document).ready(function () {
			// 
			$("a.Menu").each(function () {
				this.href = "" + this.getAttribute("href", 2); // get rid of the link completely
				this.href = this.href.replace("https", "http");
			});
			// 


			$('.topLangInfoFlag').click(function (e) {
				SetLanguage(e);
				// LangDialogDiv.dialog("open");
				return false;
			});
			$(".flag_icon_" + "en").css("border-color", "#FCB99C");	// change border on current lang flags to the the selected color

			LangSelectForm = $("#LangSelectForm");
			/******
			LangDialogDiv = $("#topLangPopup");
			LangInfoDiv = $("#topLangInfoCurrent");
			LangDialog = LangDialogDiv.dialog({
				autoOpen: false,
				modal: true,
				dialogClass: "LangDialog",
				closeText: "",
				width: "200", height: "75",
				position: { my: 'left top', at: 'left bottom', of: $("#topLangInfoCurrent") },
				resizable: false, draggable: false,
				buttons: {
					"Select Language": function () { SetLanguage(); },
					Cancel: function () { LangDialog.dialog("close"); }
				},
				show: { effect: "blind", duration: 200 },
				hide: { effect: "blind", duration: 200 }
			});
			$('#topLangInfoCurrent').click(function () {
				LangDialogDiv.dialog("open");
				return false;
			});
			******/
		});

		function SetLanguage(e) {
			// alert("Your language has been set to: " + $("#LanguageTag").val());
			var flagLangTagClass = e.currentTarget.classList[1];	// dangerously assuming that the identifying class is always the second one in the class attribute
			var langtag = flagLangTagClass.replace("flag_icon_", "")

			// swap borders
			$(".topLangInfoFlag").css("border-color", "#FEFBF6");	// all set to the background color
			$("." + flagLangTagClass).css("border-color", "#FCB99C");	// the selected color

			$("#LanguageTag").val(langtag);
			$("#LangChanged").val("1");
			//LangDialog.dialog("close");
			LangSelectForm.submit();	// this will redraw the page....
		}
	</script>
</body>
